Pan Gongzhan and Chu Minyi took the night express train to Beijing yesterday. Zhang Zhijiang and Lü Chao took the night express train from Beijing yesterday and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

The First Lottery for the Unified Public Bonds A and B Was Held Yesterday Morning; the Lotteries for C, D, and E Bonds Are Scheduled for June and July; Redemption of Winning Bonds and Discounting of Due Interest Coupons Will Be Handled by the Three Banks Simultaneously Starting at the End of July 102

The first lottery for the Republic of China 25th Year Unified Public Bonds A and B was held at 10:00 AM yesterday at the Bankers' Association at 59 Hong Kong Road. Five bonds of each type were drawn, for a total principal redemption of 1.5 million yuan. The lotteries for Bonds C and D are scheduled for June, and the lottery for Bond E is scheduled for July. Redemption for all five types will begin simultaneously on July 31st. An agreement has been reached with the Central Bank, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications regarding the discounting and rediscounting of winning bonds and due interest coupons. Details are as follows:

Attendees

The attendees included Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department of the Ministry of Finance; Lin Jinyu, Supervisor from the Auditing Department; Xu Jiyin, from the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce; Fan Jietang, from the National Debt Fund Management Committee; Wu Yunzhai, from the Shanghai Bankers' Association; Liu Wuqiao, from the Shanghai Native Bankers' Association; Jin Wenyuan, from the Central Bank; Zhu Qizhen, from the Bank of China; Chen Jun, from the Bank of Communications; He Xiaojuan, Zong Boxuan, and Liang Yaozongfa, the managers; Yun Dunzi, Ji Juncai, and Fang Jingzhong, the registrars; Wang Huaifen, Huang Qiliang, Ling Qixun, and Huang Meizhao, the document officers; Gong Baozhen, Zheng Yijian, Chen Jian, and Xu Bangzheng, the receptionists; and Lu Shuping from the Shanghai Municipal Government and Luo Quyu from the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, totaling more than thirty people.

Chairman's Report

Jiang Lufu, Director of the Public Debt Department and Chairman, reported that today is the first lottery for the redemption of the Republic of China 25th Year Unified Public Bonds A and B. The lottery method used is to draw bonds with the same last three digits. The quota for each of the two types of bonds is 150 million yuan. This time, five bonds of each type will be drawn for redemption, with a principal redemption of 750,000 yuan for each type. The payment of principal and due interest for all winning bonds will be made by the Central Bank and its authorized agents, the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications, starting on July 31st in various locations. Furthermore, in order to facilitate the financing needs of bondholders, the Ministry has obtained the right to rediscount the aforementioned winning bonds and interest coupons due at the end of July with the Central Bank, or to discount them with the Bank of China and the Bank of Communications. This matter was communicated to the three banks on February 15, 25th year. With the report completed, please have the supervisors check the lottery branches and the lottery branch register in order to proceed with the lottery.

Winning Numbers

After the chairman finished his report, the supervisors checked the lottery branches and the register, and then the lottery was conducted. The five winning numbers for Bond A are 109, 217, 355, 473, and 736. The five winning numbers for Bond B are 117, 262, 483, 696, and 704. The results will be announced by the Ministry of Finance on the same day for public knowledge.

The Social Bureau Instructs All Trade Associations to Re-Elect According to the Law 105

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau instructed the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday: "The Municipal Government's Instruction No. 17834 states that the Ministry of Industry's Consultation No. 42245 states that Article 19 of the Chamber of Commerce Law regarding the term of office of committee members also applies to industry and commerce associations. In the past, there have been delays in re-elections of merchant organizations in various places, and the Ministry has repeatedly notified the provincial and municipal governments to instruct them to re-elect within the time limit, without delay. It has been found that there are still a few chambers of commerce and industry and commerce associations that have failed to hold re-elections on schedule, which is inconsistent with the law. The local competent authorities should be responsible for investigating and supervising the process. If the re-election is still delayed, it should be handled in accordance with Article 19 of the Implementation Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law, in order to emphasize commercial operations and comply with the law. In addition to consulting, we respectfully request you to investigate and instruct compliance. We have instructed the Chamber of Commerce to comply with the provisions of the Ministry of Industry’s Commercial Letter No. 24917. Therefore, the Bureau instructs the Chamber to comply and also instruct the affiliated trade associations who have not held re-elections as scheduled to hold re-elections according to law as soon as possible, without further delay, this is of utmost importance."

Superstitious Person's Strange Behavior: Hiding Erotic Pictures to Suppress Evil Magic? 114

Chen Hairong, a 38-year-old man from Yangzhou, who lives at 3620 Yinghua Lane, Shanghai West, makes a living by working. According to Chen's confession, he had returned to his hometown earlier because of an incident, and suddenly found that the money and other items in his leather suitcase had been stolen on the ship, while the suitcase remained. He was greatly shocked. Later, a fellow passenger said that it was stolen by the iron abacus (meaning the so-called evil magic that steals property in superstitious society). Completely Eliminating Opium Addiction: Citywide General Crackdown Begins Today; the Municipal Government and the Crackdown Commissioner Jointly Issue a Proclamation; Crackdown Commissioner Ma Liang Rushes to Shanghai to Preside Over the Work; Registration for Opium Addicts Is Still Allowed During the Crackdown Period 115

The Dagong News Agency reports that the crackdown on opium addiction and the registration of opium addicts in this city have been jointly proclaimed by the municipal government and the Opium Prohibition Commissioner's Office of the Military Commission, and will be implemented starting today, with the crackdown period ending on August 10th of this year. If any opium addicts are found after the deadline, they will be sentenced to death or life imprisonment. Crackdown Commissioner Ma Liang of the Military Commission rushed to Shanghai last night to preside over the opium prohibition work. Details are as follows:

Joint Proclamation

The Shanghai Municipal Government and the Opium Addict Registration and Opium Prohibition Crackdown Commissioner's Office of the Jiangsu Province and Shanghai Municipality of the Military Commission jointly proclaimed that the opium prohibition crackdown in this city has been decided upon and will be implemented from May 10th to August 10th of this year. During this period, anyone who is addicted to opium who requests self-reform from the Municipal Public Security Bureau will be sent to the temporary drug rehabilitation center for treatment, and will be exempt from criminal penalties. If they continue to be stubborn and unrepentant, they will be severely punished according to the law if they are discovered. In addition to ordering the Public Security Bureau to comply, we hereby issue a joint proclamation for general knowledge. Mayor Wu Tiecheng and Opium Prohibition Commissioner Ma Liang.

Ma's Arrival in Shanghai

Ma Liang, the Opium Addiction Crackdown Commissioner for Jiangsu and Shanghai Municipality, specially appointed by the Opium Prohibition Supervisory Department of the Military Commission, came to Shanghai last week to inspect the opium addiction situation in this city and, after meeting with the authorities, went to Zhen and then to Beijing to report the situation to the Opium Prohibition General Association of the Military Commission. The crackdown in Shanghai is scheduled to begin today, so Ma rushed to Shanghai last night to preside over the general crackdown on opium addict registration and opium prohibition in Shanghai.

Opium Prohibition Crackdown

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau announced that the Municipal Government's Instruction No. 18283 states that the Municipal Government has issued the Opium Prohibition Crackdown Measures and ordered the Municipal Government to work with the Opium Prohibition Commissioner to implement the measures. The Municipal Government has consulted with the Opium Addict Registration Commissioner and the Opium Prohibition Crackdown Commissioner's Office and decided that the opium prohibition crackdown period will be from May 10th to August 10th. During this period, anyone who is addicted to morphine, red pills, and other highly addictive drugs who reports to the Bureau and requests self-reform will be sent to the temporary drug rehabilitation center and exempted from criminal penalties. The Municipal Treasury will be responsible for all expenses, and no fees will be charged. This is the last opportunity for opium addicts to reform themselves. If they continue to be stubborn and unrepentant, they will be severely punished according to the law by the Songhu Garrison Headquarters if they are discovered after the crackdown period. It should be noted that the Provisional Regulations for the Prohibition of Opium and Punishment of Crimes are extremely strict. All criminals who manufacture, sell, or traffic in drugs will be sentenced to death and their property confiscated. Opium addicts who do not voluntarily quit will be sentenced to imprisonment of not less than three years if they are discovered within this year, in addition to being ordered to quit. In the 26th year of the Republic, anyone who uses opium or injects morphine privately will be sentenced to death or life imprisonment. The crackdown period is only three months, and it will pass quickly. All those who are addicted to drugs should go for rehabilitation as soon as possible and should not test the law with their own bodies and regret it later. This is of utmost importance. This is hereby announced. May 10, 25th year of the Republic of China. Director Cai Jingjun.

Opium Addiction Crackdown

It has been decided in this city that the period from May 10th to August 10th is the deadline for registration of opium addicts. During this period, opium addicts who have not registered are allowed to register retroactively, pay fees, and receive licenses, and will not be punished. All opium addicts who have failed to register should be awakened and take this last opportunity to register retroactively with the Bureau. If they still intend to evade and wait and see, they will still be sent to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for punishment in accordance with the Provisional Regulations for the Prohibition of Opium and Punishment of Crimes after the crackdown period expires, without any leniency. Do not mislead yourselves again. In addition to ordering the branch bureaus and offices to comply, we are appending the procedures for retroactive registration for opium addicts during the crackdown period for general knowledge.

Retroactive Registration

The Municipal Public Security Bureau has stipulated the following procedures for retroactive registration for opium addicts during the crackdown period: Registration of opium addicts will be carried out from May 10th to August 10th of this year. If registration is not completed after the deadline, punishment will be imposed in accordance with the Provisional Regulations for the Prohibition of Opium and Punishment of Crimes once it is discovered. Those who register and apply for an ordinary opium addiction cessation license must pay a license fee of 5 yuan. Those who register and apply for a poor opium addiction cessation license must pay a license fee of 6 jiao. For opium addicts who have previously failed to register, during the crackdown registration period, they should obtain a retroactive registration application form for ordinary licenses from the local Public Security Bureau and team. If they are applying for a poor license, in addition to applying for a poor license application form, they must also provide a guarantee letter, and fill in the required information separately, together with the license fee, and apply for registration. Anyone who has relatives, friends, or neighbors can act as a guarantor for the poor opium addict. There is no need for a shop to act as a guarantor. Opium addicts who have registered and obtained a license certificate must, within one month after half a month, take it to the original registration authority to exchange it for a license. Opium addicts living in the Special District may apply directly to the Bureau or to the nearby Public Security Branch Office for registration, and must clearly state their Chinese communication address in the application form. Opium addicts who apply for free opium addiction cessation during the opium addict registration period should fill out an application for opium addiction cessation and a guarantee letter, and submit them to the Bureau or each branch bureau and team, and wait for regular transfer for opium addiction cessation. If there is no guarantor, they can also apply to the branch bureau for transfer to the Bureau for transfer to opium addiction cessation. When applying for registration, opium addicts should report their true name, age, and address. If they fabricate any information, their application for retroactive registration will be rejected once the investigation confirms the falsehood.

Mobilization in All Districts

The branch bureaus and offices of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau have received instructions from the General Bureau that the opium prohibition crackdown and opium addict registration in this city will begin today. In order to make all opium addicts in the city generally understand the importance of this general crackdown and to prevent opium addicts from being negligent and committing crimes, the Bureau has ordered each branch bureau and office to organize a persuasion team and to mobilize the whole city to distribute leaflets on the procedures for retroactive registration for opium addicts during the crackdown period to each household.

The Suspect Tang Zhouer, Who Assaulted a Japanese Constable, Is Under Investigation; He Could Not See the Face Clearly in the Dark; The Injury on His Middle Finger Was Said to Be a Scratch from the Rickshaw Handle 116

At 8:30 PM on the 30th of last month, a Japanese constable No. 139 from the Huishan Police Station was on duty on Huishan Road when he was suddenly dragged to a remote area by four people who looked like rickshaw pullers. Two people held him down, and one person covered his mouth with his hand, intending to snatch his gun. The Japanese constable shouted, bit the person's finger, and managed to break free. He blew his whistle and used his right hand to draw his gun for self-defense. One person stabbed him twice in the back of his hand with a knife, and his left hand was also injured by a knife. At this time, Chinese constable No. 1741 and other Japanese constables heard the alarm and arrived, and the group dispersed, losing a whistle. The Japanese constable was sent to the hospital for treatment, and his injuries were minor. He was discharged the next day. The Chinese and Western detectives of the police station conducted investigations, but could not find any clues. At about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Chinese detective Ya Yonglu received a report from Qian that Tang Zhouer, a rickshaw puller from Tongzhou living at No. 19 Huaji Road, was highly suspected. So he secretly went to the address and arrested him, confiscating a small knife and a set of muddy short-sleeved shirt and pants, and brought him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the Special First Court. The engineer and lawyer Li Zhishan explained the case and said that Tang had been prosecuted four times for theft and robbery, but he did not admit to the crime in the police station. Please detain him for further investigation. Detective Ya reported the process, and presented the small knife, short-sleeved shirt and pants, and a felt hat left by the group at the scene of the incident for inspection. The Japanese constable said that it was dark at the open space at that time, and he could not see the faces of the four people clearly. The arrested defendant seemed to be the person who covered his mouth with his hand. Tang Erjian did not admit it, and said that there was indeed a wound on the middle finger of his right hand, which was scratched on the rickshaw handle three days ago. The muddy short-sleeved shirt and pants were worn on rainy days. He asked for identification. Judge Jiang ordered him to be detained for further investigation and verification.

The Murderer of Ye Ganxiu, Wu Zhiguang, Confessed After Initial Interrogation; Handgun Coated with Red Cement Because His Brother-in-Law Colluded with Officials to Bully Him 117

Last month, on the 4th, a shooting occurred in Gan County, Jiangxi Province. The deceased was named Ye Ganxiu. After investigation by the Gan County Local Court Prosecutor's Office, the identified perpetrators were Wu Zhiguang, a native of Guangdong and Ye's brother-in-law, and a man named Li Defang. Arrest warrants were issued. On April 9th, Li Defang was apprehended by the authorities. A savings passbook under the name of Wu Zhiguang at the Shanghai Juxingcheng Bank, No. 2883, was confiscated, with a balance of 850 yuan. The Gan County Prosecutor's Office immediately sent a letter to the Shanghai Juxingcheng Bank, requesting that if anyone came to inquire about or withdraw money using the passbook, they should be detained and handed over to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for custody. Upon receiving the letter, the bank instructed its staff to pay attention. The afternoon before yesterday, the principal offender in the case, Wu Zhiguang, suddenly arrived at the Juxingcheng Bank, claiming that the passbook had been lost and wanting to withdraw money. Because the bank staff did not remember the Gan County public letter, they asked Wu to leave a signature sample and to publish a declaration in the newspaper. Wu then left the bank. Wu gave his address as Room 332, Asia Hotel, 153 Avenue Edward VII. When the bank remembered, Wu had already left. The bank drafted a letter together with the public letter from the Gan County Local Court Prosecutor's Office and sent it to the General Inspectorate. Detective Li Jincheng and Western Detective Chief Tielerden rushed to Room 332 of the Asia Hotel and arrested Wu. Wu confessed that he killed [Ye Ganxiu] out of resentment because his brother-in-law, Ye Ganxiu, had colluded with the local Public Security Bureau chief to bully [Wu]. After the incident, he threw the handgun into the river. The detectives did not believe that he had thrown the handgun away. Under strict questioning, Wu confessed that the gun had not been discarded, but was wrapped in cloth and coated with red cement after the incident. The detectives searched the room and found the handgun covered in red cement and brought it back to the station. Yesterday, [Wu] was sent to the First Special District Court, Criminal Division One. The police lawyer Wang Yaotang explained the situation and requested a ruling. Interrogated, Wu Zhiguang admitted to shooting and killing Ye Ganxiu. Judge Feng Shide verified the confession and ordered the case to be adjourned, pending notification to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office to send personnel to receive the case.

In the Case of the Assassination of a Japanese Sailor, Ye Haisheng Also Accused Zhou Sherong; Police Prevented Retraction and Sent for Interrogation; Ye Even Described the Situation When Drawing Lots, Zhou Sherong Absolutely Denied Any Knowledge 123

After Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo was shot and killed on Avenue Doumer on the evening of November 9th last year, the Public Concession Police Department arrested four people: Korean Jack (Chinese name Han Qiliang), and Cantonese Yang Wendao, Chen Rongsheng, and Ye Haisheng (also known as Xiao Guangdong). Jack was sent to the Japanese Consulate, Chen Rongsheng was released due to lack of evidence, and Yang and Ye were prosecuted by the Shanghai Municipal Council Legal Department on charges of murder. The First Special District Court held two public hearings on the matter, as detailed in this newspaper. The afternoon before yesterday, Ye Haisheng also confessed to the police that a Cantonese man, Zhou Sherong (also known as Yaorong, Da Zhou, Ya Zhou, 30 years old, resident of No. 13 Dade Lane, North Sichuan Road), was also present when Yang Wendao and others were discussing the assassination of Nakayama Hideo at the Tongyi Xie [Association]. Zhou is currently working as an inspector at the Dalu Ballroom at No. 33 Ningbo Road. According to the confession, the police arrested Zhou at the Dalu Ballroom at 11:00 PM the night before last, led by Western Detective Chief Ke Laote and Losi, and sent him to the First Special District Court Criminal Division One at 11:05 AM yesterday morning. Judge Feng Shide, accompanied by clerk Ding Chongnan, took the bench and questioned [Zhou]. After asking the suspect Zhou about his age, residence, and occupation, police lawyer Wang Yaotang stood up and stated that the suspect Zhou Sherong was suspected of being involved in the case of the assassination of Japanese sailor Nakayama Hideo. Co-offender Ye Haisheng confessed that Zhou was also present when [they] were discussing the assassination of Nakayama Hideo at the Tongyi Xie [Association] at No. 71 Yongji Lane on Bazilu before implementing it. Therefore, the police's Western Detectives Ke Laote and Losi arrested Zhou at the Dalu Ballroom last night. First, [he was] taken to the Chengdu Road police station, where Ye Haisheng confronted him. At that time, in addition to the two Western detectives and the deputy chief, Chinese Detective Chief Xue Zhiqian was also present. The police now need to thoroughly investigate whether Zhou is definitely related to this case, so according to Articles 76 and 101 of the Criminal Procedure Law, the court is requested to approve the detention. If it is believed that Zhou definitely has criminal facts, [he] will be prosecuted together with Yang Wendao and others on the 20th of this month. And today Ye Haisheng has also brought to the case, in order to prevent repudiation, the court should first interrogate Ye, etc.. Then Western Detective Chief Ke Laote reported the circumstances of Zhou's arrest, saying that Ye had previously confessed that Zhou was present at the meeting, and confessed it again yesterday, so the police went to the Dalu Ballroom and arrested him. The court then questioned Zhou, "Do you know Yang Wendao, Ye Haisheng, and Han Qiliang?" [Zhou] answered, "I know them all." [The court] asked, "Are you a member of the Tongyi Xie [Association]?" [Zhou] answered, "Yes." [The court] asked, "Have you ever participated in discussing the assassination of a Japanese sailor?" [Zhou] answered, "I know nothing about this matter at all." The court then summoned Ye Haisheng to the witness stand. According to Ye's confession, "I have known Zhou Sherong for a long time. Zhou was also present when [we] were discussing at the Tongyi Xie [Association], and I was also called there by Zhou. The first time was on October 2nd or 3rd, Zhou went to the Yuegong Ballroom and called me to the Tongyi Xie to meet Yang Wendao and the two Koreans, one of whom was Jack. Because I had fought with Jack before, I was not happy about it. Yang knew what was on my mind and said that now that Zhou had introduced [us], [we] should get along well in the future and not argue anymore, and that many Koreans would join the association as members in the future. At the end of October, Zhou came to the Yuegong again and called me to the Tongyi Xie. I went with him. According to Yang Wendao, [we] were preparing to kill a Japanese person and asked me if I agreed. Zhou and I both expressed our agreement. A Korean said that he could prepare handguns, etc. Yang said that [we] also had them. Later, [we] went to Avenue Sayle to scout the route. On the 8th, Yang took out four paper rolls, three of which were blank, and one had the word "go" written on it. He ordered me, Zhou, and the two Koreans to each draw one. I drew a paper roll with the word "go" on it. This task was then assigned to me. Because Yang was the chairman of the association, he did not draw a roll. On the evening of the 9th, at 8:00 PM, [we] set off together. Yang was afraid that too many people would spoil things, so he instructed Zhou not to go. When [we] arrived at the Dongyang School, Yang handed me a handgun. I then proceeded to Avenue Doumer to wait. Soon, I saw Yang and others coming along behind a Japanese sailor. Yang signaled to me with his mouth, saying that the person to be killed was this person. I closely followed the sailor to near the Fengle Lane and then shot him. After the incident, I returned to the Yuegong and met Zhou. Zhou asked me how things were going. I told him that it was done. This is the beginning and end of the matter. At that time, according to Yang, the person they wanted to kill was a Japanese military officer, etc." Judge Feng immediately asked Zhou if what Ye had said was correct. Zhou shook his head repeatedly, saying that he knew nothing about this matter at all and had not participated in any discussions. He also said that he knew nothing about Ye's confession of joint agreement and drawing lots. The court asked if he had any animosity with Ye. [Zhou] answered that [they] had no animosity at all. At this point, it was 11:40 AM. Judge Feng then ordered that Zhou Sherong be detained. If the police investigation reveals no criminal suspicion by the afternoon of the 20th of this month, [he] should be released from custody in advance. The court then adjourned, and the two offenders, Ye and Zhou, were escorted back to the police station for detention by four Japanese police officers and Chinese and Western detectives.

Women's Cooperative

To promote women's economic independence, 3. To advocate production cooperation, and 4. To serve the community. The cooperative has the following departments: 1. Food Department, including Chinese and Western refreshments, sanitary lunch boxes, sweets, and biscuits, 2. Handicraft Department, including clothing, food supplies, household items, and children's supplies, and 3. U.S. Navy Personnel Stationed in Shanghai Celebrating Mother's Day Today 125

The Greater Shanghai Evening Post reported that tomorrow (the 10th), personnel from the U.S. Fourth Marine Regiment and the U.S. Asiatic Fleet stationed in Shanghai will observe Mother's Day. A special prayer meeting will be held at the Grand Theatre at 10:30 AM, with sermons by U.S. clergy, Mrs. Lawsonfelt, etc., singing, and music provided by the Fourth Marine Regiment and the Lancashire Regiment. Many American families in Shanghai will also follow customs and entertain soldiers. The U.S. Navy YMCA will also hold a meeting to celebrate. It is said that Mother's Day was founded in 1906 by Ms. Jarvis of Philadelphia and has now been widely adopted throughout the country. All states have a day off on this day, and all schools, churches, and social organizations observe it. People in the U.S. Army, Navy, and Marine Corps attach great importance to this holiday. All those serving abroad who have mothers at home send letters or telegrams on this day to express their filial thoughts.

Dangerous Hidden Reef Discovered at the Mouth of the Qiantang River in Hangzhou; Only Six Feet Below the Water Surface, the Situation is Dangerous; Hydrographic Office Warns of Navigation Attention 128

The naval vessel of the Hydrographic Office in this city discovered a reef at the mouth of the Qiantang River in Hangzhou, only six feet below the water surface, posing an extremely dangerous situation. Yesterday, a warning was issued, ordering the navigation industry to pay attention. The details are recorded below.

Reef Discovered

After discovering the hidden reef at the mouth of the Qiantang River in Hangzhou Bay, the Hydrographic Office immediately sent a surveying vessel to conduct sounding. The results showed that its position was at 120 degrees 59 minutes east longitude and approximately 30 degrees 28 minutes north latitude. The depth of the reef from the water surface is six feet, posing a dangerous situation. Therefore, the bureau specially warned the navigation industry to pay attention yesterday.

Suspension of Navigation

At the same time, the bureau also reported according to the report from the Guangzhou Port Director, the waterway in the Zhujiang River basin, named Niugu Sha South (approximately 113 degrees east longitude, 23 degrees 7 minutes north latitude), is now temporarily closed to navigation due to the start of construction of the southwest railway bridge. According to the report, the bureau also notified the various shipping companies yesterday, ordering them to be informed.

Ningbo Natives Abroad Are Concerned About the Issue of Tomb Relocation; Letters to Shanghai Fellow Townsmen's Association Urging Them to Persist in Taking Charge 129

Since the various counties and towns of Ningbo Prefecture have been carrying out the demolition of tombs within a limited time, the news has spread far and wide. Ningbo natives abroad are all alarmed and at a loss. This is because Ningbo people are devoted to filial piety, and tomb sweeping during Qingming is a common practice. Once the ancestral tombs are suddenly demolished, it is appropriate for them to be heartbroken and to think of exerting all their strength to fight for it. It is heard that Ningbo natives abroad are extremely concerned about this case and have repeatedly urged the Shanghai Fellow Townsmen's Association to firmly take charge. Here is a letter from the Luxun Fellow Townsmen's Association to the association, which shows a glimpse of [the situation]. The letter says, "It has been found that the various counties of our Ningbo Prefecture have recently received orders from the county government to demolish graves within a limited time. The time is urgent, and the ancestral tombs of those who are not able to return to their hometowns to handle [the matter] in time, and those who are unemployed in their hometowns and unable to relocate [the tombs] in time, are in danger of being forcibly demolished. It is also heard that in the Cixi area along the railway, the statistics of the expenses of those who own tombs and comply with the order to demolish [them] this time are about more than one million. At a time when the countryside is bankrupt and industry and commerce are declining, the necessary food and clothing expenses for people's lives are not enough, and forcing them to relocate ancestral tombs suddenly adds a burden, it is no wonder that people are resentful and complaints are heard everywhere. Recently, [we] heard that you, gentlemen of the association, are concerned about your hometown and have sent telegrams to the provincial government and President Chiang, requesting the correction of methods, the gradual implementation, the consideration of the suffering of the people, and the benevolence to the withered bones underground. Your benevolence and righteous deeds are admirable. We hope that you will persevere in taking charge and will not stop until you reach your goal. We are very fortunate, yours sincerely, the Luxun Fellow Townsmen."

Zheng Shixi Lost His Job and Jumped Off a Building; Fractured His Left Foot and Shattered His Skull 130

Zheng Shixi, a 25-year-old man from Nanjing, is staying at the New Era Dance School, which his brother established, at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Danshui Road. Gave Birth to Daughter Two Years Ago, Now Pregnant Again: Female Servant Accuses of Seduction and Abandonment; Pan Yilan Lives Affluently, Judge Advises Reconciliation 132

Pan Yaoting and his son Pan Yilan, both locals from No. 133 Lichuan Lane, Dongjiadu, Nanshi, are in the financial industry and work at the Sino-French Savings Bank. Their occupations are respectable, and their lives are affluent. Recently, Lu Shizhen, their former female servant (i.e., the eldest sister), 26 years old, from Songjiang, accused Pan Yilan of seduction and abandonment, and also implicated Pan's colleague, Wang Tianyou, in helping with intimidation and forcing her to sign a severance agreement. Yesterday at 5:15 PM, Presiding Judge Cai opened the court to hear the case. Lu Shizhen, represented by lawyers Chen Heting and Xu Lin, claimed that on February 12th of the 23rd year of the Republic [1934], she was introduced by Aunt Xu to work as a servant in Pan Yaoting's home. The young master, Pan Yilan, saw that the plaintiff was young and falsely claimed that his wife had run off with another man, and wanted her to become his mistress. Pan Yaoting also testified that his daughter-in-law had left, and no one was taking care of his grandson, Little Rabbit, so he encouraged them to be together. After six or seven days, he asked an old matchmaker to propose marriage. She mistakenly believed their words and began cohabiting with him. On the sixth day of the first month of the 24th year [1935], she gave birth to a daughter named Mina, who is now two years old, and is currently three months pregnant again. On October 12th of the same year, they moved to No. 12 Jishan Lane, Zhabu Road, and lived there until December 27th, when someone brought several people to move away their belongings and tried to steal her daughter. Fortunately, the landlord helped her avoid this. Then, Wang Tianyou came to intimidate her, demanding a severance of their relationship, or she would face three and a half years of litigation. Defendant Pan Yaoting testified that he did not know about his son's affair. Lu Shizhen was temporarily out of work. The judge said that regardless of whether the criminal charges are established, since a child has been born, raising the child is just. Reconciliation is the best course of action. He asked why Pan Yilan was not present and ordered him to be brought to court for questioning next time. Pan Yaoting complied. The judge also questioned Wang Tianyou, and ordered him to be summoned again later.

Renting a Room, Using a Fake Gun to Rob; Old Woman Urgently Shouts "Catch the Thief!"; Police Detectives Arrive, Thieves Disappear Without a Trace 141

Zheng Rongting, 30 years old, a local resident of No. 1 Fangxie Lane, Fangxie Road, Nanshi, runs a foreign goods business. Because he has a spare attic room, he put it up for rent. At about 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, two men wearing blue cloth long gowns and short jackets, speaking in a local accent, knocked on the door and entered, pretending to rent the room. They agreed to rent the attic room for seven yuan per month and paid a deposit of one yuan, saying that they would come tomorrow to wallpaper the room. After speaking, they left. Yesterday afternoon at about 2:30 PM, two men indeed came carrying a roll of patterned paper and went upstairs to wallpaper. Soon, one person went out to buy more paper and came back. Seeing that there was only an old woman (i.e., Zheng Rongting's mother-in-law), Ms. Wang, doing needlework in the living room, the thief took out a gun from his sleeve, threatened her to keep silent, and forced Ms. Wang to hand over her jewelry. Ms. Wang shouted, "Catch the thief!" At the same time, a thief upstairs also came downstairs. Seeing that the old woman was shouting, the thieves pushed Ms. Wang to the ground in a panic and fled. The patrol police nearby heard the shout and reported to the Ximen Branch Bureau. Bureau officer Huang Tizhi led a large number of police detectives to pursue the thieves. The thieves, unable to rob, dropped a fake gun and escaped through the back door without a trace.

China First Knitting Factory Investigates Counterfeit Trademarks; Four Criminals Have Been Detained in Succession; Handed Over to the General Bureau for Investigation 143

The Shanghai China First Knitting Factory, located at Zhongtai'an Lane, the intersection of Sichuan Road and Ningbo Road, has been established for many years. The factory's Ink Chrysanthemum brand socks are sold in various ports, and the business is booming. Recently, counterfeit products have been found on the market, and dealers from other ports have sent letters suspecting the factory of mixing inferior goods, which has greatly affected the business. The factory owner sent people to investigate. Yesterday afternoon, it was learned that the Xincheng Printing Bureau at No. 8 Ningkang Lane, Anlan Road, Ximen, specializes in printing counterfeit trademarks. They went to investigate and found seven counterfeit printing plates inside. They arrested a shop assistant, Yang Boliang, and took him and the printing plates to the Ximen Branch Bureau, accusing the bureau of printing counterfeit trademarks for use on inferior socks to impersonate the products of the China First Knitting Factory, deceiving customers who came to question them. Bureau Chief Huang interrogated Yang, who claimed that the printing of the counterfeit trademarks was arranged by the boss, Jin Zupei. He was evasive about the rest. Later, the detective squad leader Li Xiaoshi sent personnel to secretly arrest Jin and confiscated 100,500 printed counterfeit trademarks. It was learned that the counterfeit trademarks were commissioned by Yang Ruijin of the Xinhua Printing Office at No. 99 Siwen Lane, Xinzha. Yang was arrested. Yang confessed that he was instructed by Li Zaixian, a Shanxi native of the Li Yu National Goods Store at No. 27 Shengping Lane, Avenue Edward VII. The team sent Jin Yushan and Chen Minsheng, along with the French Concession Police, to search the Li Yu Store and seized hundreds of counterfeit trademarks and four pairs of white socks mixed with inferior goods, pretending to be Ink Chrysanthemum brand. Li Zaixian was arrested. The interrogation involved many people. Because the case involved counterfeiting trademarks, the four arrested criminals and more than 100,000 counterfeit trademarks were transferred to the General Bureau for investigation.

Establishment of the Qingliang Temple Maintenance Association; Wang Yiting, etc., Elected as Standing Committee Members; Association Headquarters Established in the Chinese Buddhist Association on Hart Road 144

The Dagong Society, the Qingliang Temple on Xinzha Road, is a famous temple in Shanghai. Recently, due to land disputes, litigation has been ongoing for years. Although the court has ruled for enforcement, the matter is still difficult to resolve. Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Zhu Qinglan, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Huang Jinrong, Pan Gongzhan, Wu Xingya, Cai Jinjun, etc., in order to respect religion and protect the temple, have repeatedly held discussions to maintain it and have received assistance from various parties. However, due to the lack of a fixed organization, progress has been inconvenient. Therefore, they have solicited support from all sectors to jointly launch the "Shanghai Qingliang Temple Maintenance Association" with the aim of settling disputes peacefully, resolving difficulties, eliminating obstacles to understanding with affection, and complementing the shortcomings of the law with public opinion, so that both parties can achieve fairness and success will not be quickly destroyed. The Maintenance Association convened an inaugural meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday on the ninth floor of the YMCA of Eight Immortals Bridge, announcing its official establishment. More than 100 people attended, including Huang Jinrong, Zhu Qinglan, Yuan Ludeng, Wang Yiting, Wu Tiecheng, Li Dachao, Jiang Kanghu, Qu Yingguang, Yang Hu (Wang Ji-yi representing him), etc. The meeting passed five articles of association: 1. The association is named the Shanghai Qingliang Temple Maintenance Association. 2. The association is solely responsible for mediation and relief in the Qingliang Temple litigation, with the aim of maintaining the existence of the temple. 3. The association is launched by the Qingliang Temple's benefactors and patrons over the years. Anyone who expresses sympathy for this matter can join as a member. 4. Members of the association will elect officials, who will fulfill their obligations without remuneration. 5. The association will elect several standing committee members to preside over the affairs of the association. Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Shichang, Li Dachao, Qu Yingguang, Jiang Kanghu, Yang Shunquan, Li Binsen, Yuan Xi tao, Wang Ji-yi, Xin Shude, Chen Fukang, Cao Mingwei, Lu Qi, and Zhang Xuxian were elected as standing committee members on the spot. It was also resolved to establish the association's headquarters in the Chinese Buddhist Association on Hart Road in the Western District of Shanghai. Finally, Yuan Ludeng, Li Dachao, and others expressed their opinions one after another. Jiang Kanghu also stood up and reported that a Westerner named Du Daqun, who had joined the association, claimed that Tonghe Foreign Firm's foreigner Mr. Seger was not in charge of the Qingliang Temple's land mortgage. It was rumored that the land had not been mortgaged. After mutual discussion, they unanimously advocated two measures: 1. To request an extension of the deadline for the execution of the land mortgage; 2. To assess the land price, raise funds, and find a way to recover it. The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM.

Since Mr. Shao Runing reorganized and expanded the Shanghai Jiren Aid Material Association and began soliciting new members, in just one week, the number of applicants has doubled. Once the first group of 500 Ren [benevolence] units is fully subscribed, membership reports will be distributed, and the solicitation of the second group of Yi [righteousness] units will continue. In the future, the work of all five groups of Ren, Yi, Li [rites], Zhi [wisdom], and Xin [trustworthiness] will be completed with 2,500 units fully subscribed. The material production site has been selected at No. 128 Gonghe Xin Road, Zhabei, a huge building, and the public cemetery and Yi [righteousness] cemetery have also been selected at Beixinjing and Dachang, both covering more than 10 mu [~0.67 hectares]. The basic quota of 400 sets of material (each set costing 25 yuan) has been subscribed to by Mr. Weng Gang of Siemens, Lu Yunxiang of the Pioneer Company's Leather Goods Department, Zheng Legeng, Zhang Jialiu, and others. The remaining are still being solicited. The association's headquarters has been moved from Nine Acres Land to No. 6 Dakang Lane, Bair Road, French Concession (telephone 80419). It is not difficult to count the days until the solicitation goal is reached.

Request to Improve the Official Documents for Appeal Case Fee Payment Method 152

Lawyer Qu Yue and other members of the Shanghai Lawyers Association, due to the inconvenience of the Civil Appeal Court's refusal to accept trial fees and the requirement to submit receipts, made a suggestion requesting transfer for improvement. The conference decided to transfer it to the Judicial Administration Department for adoption. After the submission, the Judicial Administration Department replied that regarding the third instance appeal fee, it had been approved by the Supreme Court, and a separate method had been established, which should be followed. As for the second instance appeal fee, it would be more convenient for the party concerned to pay it to the original trial court for transfer when filing the appeal. The instructions of the Judicial Administration Department and the reply of the Supreme Court are recorded below: Judicial Administration Department Reply, January 14, 25th year. A document was submitted requesting improvement of the method for paying trial fees for appeal cases, please review and adopt it. Received. Regarding the third instance appeal fee, it has been approved by the Supreme Court, and a separate method has been established, which should be followed. After careful review, the second instance appeal fee should be paid by the party concerned when filing the appeal, and then transferred by the original trial court, which is more convenient. In addition to issuing orders to the courts of each province to comply with, a copy of the original letter from the Supreme Court is attached for notification. Approved. Supreme Court Reply to the Judicial Administration Department. Approved the public letter No. 73 from your department, regarding the Shanghai Lawyers Association Standing Committee Member Zhang Shizhao's submission, and the proposal by members Qu Yue, etc., requesting improvement of the appeal case fee payment method, and requesting approval for adoption. A copy of the original document is enclosed and sent to you for verification and reply for processing. This was approved, and it was submitted to the Civil Division of the court for discussion with the division chiefs and a reply was given. The reply states: "After the party concerned remits the third instance trial fee to this court, they should still submit the remittance voucher to the second instance court. Upon receiving the voucher, a receipt should be issued, and the case number, the name of the remitter, the amount of the remittance, the date of the remittance, and the place of the remittance (name of the bank or post office) should be clearly stated on the receipt. If it is necessary to deal with the original remittance place, they should be allowed to take the receipt to the second instance court to collect the original voucher, and return it after use." After verification, the proposal is appropriate and a reply is sent to you for your information. This is addressed to the Judicial Administration Department, from the Supreme Court.

The Equipment for the World Games is Extremely Complete 164

Havas, Berlin, 8th: The 11th Olympic Games is scheduled to begin here on August 1st. The participating countries include 53 countries, with no less than 5,500 athletes. The German authorities have built an Olympic village in the Tauberitz training ground, dedicated to athletes, which can accommodate 4,000 people. The timing equipment in the Games is extremely accurate, even to one-hundredth of a second, and can be recorded accurately. As soon as each competition is over, after twelve minutes, the judges can get the photo of the end point of the competition, with the time attached to it, without any errors. Therefore, it is impossible for judges to make mistakes. On the opening day of the conference, there will be 10,000 children singing Beethoven's Ninth Symphony in the field to entertain the guests. Torches will be lit all around the venue.

Features of the Soccer Special of the World Games, A Good Friend for Soccer Lovers 165

According to a Reuters dispatch from Paris, the South American Uruguayan soccer team recently toured Europe. A disturbance occurred during a match in Paris, so all European tour plans were cancelled, and they returned home immediately. Uruguay was the soccer champion team in the 1924 and 1928 Olympic Games. The depth of its soccer art has long been noticed by the soccer world. The full details of the team's victory in the soccer championship at the 9th World Games in the Netherlands in 1928 are published in the "World Games Soccer Special," edited by Shenbao reporter Jiang Huaiqing, which was recently published. The chronicle is more than 10,000 words long and is a valuable record of the world's soccer battle. Those who want to understand the true soccer skills of the Uruguayan team, the world's soccer kingdom, must read this article. The special also contains Li Huitang's "Prospects for the World Games Soccer," a brief history and photos of Chinese soccer players, and the soccer competition methods and schedule of this World Games, which is all-encompassing and beautiful. All soccer lovers must have a copy in their hands. It is beautifully printed and sells for only two dimes of ocean. The general distributor is the Sports Review Society at No. 460 Caishi Road, Shanghai. All magazine companies and newsstands on Simalu Road also sell it. Public Doubles Handball, Zhu and Sun Luckily Won Against Hua and Yan, The Result of Two Against One Was Exciting 170

The Shanghai Open Handball organized by the West Youth, Zhu Kuan and Sun Daosheng played against Hua Fenggang and Yan Peiqiu in a changed and supplementary match yesterday. At 3 o'clock, the competition began. Zhu and Sun got the serve and scored four points in a row. Yan Peiqiu pulled back one point. After several rotations, Zhu and Sun were very active and scored 11 to 1. At 14 to 4, Yan Peiqiu showed his superior skills and chased to 14 to 10. At this point, the competition between the two sides became more intense. Back and forth, after twenty meetings, Hua committed suicide with a backhand, making it 15 to 10. Zhu Kuan took the opportunity to draw the ball with the clothes line and scored four points. Although Hua and Yan made progress later, they lost too many points. They lost the first game with a score of 21 to 19. In the second game, Zhu and Sun again scored ten points in one breath. Hua and Yan worked hard and chased to 14 to 10. After this, Zhu and Sun committed suicides frequently, making it 18 to 17. Hua Peiqiu got four ball opportunities and won three points, taking the lead with 20 to 19. Zhu Kuan immediately responded, making it a tie at 20. The game was tense. Yan Peiqiu was calm in this critical moment and won the last point with a baseline corner kick, 21 to 20. Yan and Hua won the second game. At the beginning of the third game, Hua and Yan took advantage of the victory and scored seven points in a row. Until 17 to 15, the situation gradually became flat. Sun Dasheng served and scored six points in a row, 21 to 17. Yan and Hua took it again, and the result was two against one, Zhu and Sun won against Yan Peiqiu and Hua Fenggang. The three games were amazing, and the first two games were very good.

The Regular Joint Examination for High School Students in Jiangsu Province: Examinations Will Be Held at Original Schools Instead of Being Zoned; Random Examinations for Junior High School Students Will Proceed as Previously Stipulated 175

(Dispatch from Zhenjiang) It has been decided that the graduation joint examination for high school students this year will not be zoned and will be held separately at each school. The random graduation examinations for junior high school students will proceed according to the method used last year. The subjects for the high school joint examination will follow the Ministry's regulations: Chinese Language, Foreign Language, Mathematics, Science (Physics and Chemistry), and History and Geography. The date for the joint examination is set from June 22nd to June 24th of this year, and will be held simultaneously at all schools. The Department of Education has also stipulated that high school senior students who are about to graduate must make haste to complete all academic subjects. Given the limited time, schools should set their own schedules and report them to the Department for review. The provisional methods for the high school graduation joint examination and the junior high school graduation random examination are recorded below:

Methods for the High School Graduation Joint Examination

The high school graduation joint examination for this year will not be zoned and will be held separately at each school. The Department of Education will assign chief examiners and supervisors to oversee the process.

The subjects for this year's joint examination will follow the Ministry Order No. 5244: Chinese Language, Foreign Language, Mandarin Chinese, Mathematics, Science (Physics and Chemistry), and History and Geography.

The question setting and paper marking for this year's joint examination will still be handled separately by the High School Graduation Joint Examination Committee organized by the Department of Education.

The examination papers for each subject will be prepared by each school according to the format promulgated by the Department of Education (the examination paper format will be issued separately). The papers will be numbered, sealed, and stamped with the school seal. The register of secret codes should be submitted to the Department of Education for record.

The sealed papers must not be opened until after the evaluation and scoring are completed.

The joint examination is scheduled to be held simultaneously at all schools from June 22nd to June 24th. The examination timetable is as follows: (June 22nd) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Chinese Language; 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, History and Geography; (June 23rd) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Mathematics; 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, Science; (June 24th) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Foreign Language. Each subject will have three times the number of questions, and students will choose to answer one-third of them.

Each school should prepare a roster of students participating in the joint examination and a grade report of their usual performance in each subject, in the format below, 20 days before the joint examination. These, along with two 2.5-inch portrait photos of each student, with their name and age noted, should be signed and stamped by the principal for verification. (Table omitted; the student roster includes columns for academic performance, physical education performance, and conduct performance, indicating whether they passed.) (The average grade of the three academic years should be filled in for each subject.)

If a student who should participate in the graduation joint examination is temporarily unable to take the examination due to illness or special circumstances, the school may submit a request in accordance with Article 11, Section 2 of the revised regulations for the high school student graduation joint examination.

Each school should conduct the final academic year examination before the joint examination, with strict review. Those who fail the examination or do not participate in the examination will not be allowed to participate in the joint examination.

The results of the joint examination will be calculated in accordance with Article 4 of the Ministry Order No. 5244, but the order of grades will still be based on the joint examination results.

These methods are established and implemented by the Department of Education.

Methods for the Junior High School Graduation Random Examination

The subjects for the junior high school graduation random examination this year will follow the Ministry Order No. 5244: Chinese Language, Foreign Language, Mathematics, Science (Physics and Chemistry), and History and Geography.

The date for the random examination is set from June 22nd to June 24th and will be held simultaneously at all schools. The Department of Education will assign chief examiners to oversee the process.

The examination timetable for each subject of the random examination is as follows: (June 22nd) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Chinese Language; 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, History and Geography; (June 23rd) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Mathematics; 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM, Science; (June 24th) 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM, Foreign Language; 1:00 PM to 3:00 PM, Civics; 3:30 PM to 5:30 PM, Plants and Animals.

Schools subject to random examination should conduct examinations for Civics, Plants, and Animals, in addition to the random examination subjects, within the above-mentioned random examination dates and times.

Schools not subject to random examination should conduct graduation examinations for each subject within the above-mentioned random examination dates and times. Other subjects may be examined on dates determined separately by each school.

The examination questions for each subject of the random examination should first be drafted in duplicate by the teachers of each subject in each school and submitted to the principal for selection, sealing, and preservation, without prior disclosure. When the random examination takes place, the schools subject to random examination will temporarily use the examination questions brought by the chief examiners sent by the Department. Schools not subject to random examination will still use self-drafted questions.

All examination papers for each subject will be prepared by each school, numbered, sealed, and stamped with the school seal. The register of codes of numbered seals for schools subject to random examination should be submitted to the Department of Education for record.

Each school should prepare a roster of students participating in the random examination, along with two 2.5-inch portrait photos, noting the name, age, and place of origin, and signed and stamped by the principal, to be submitted to the chief examiners for verification.

After the examination is completed, the examination papers from the schools subject to random examination will be sealed by the chief examiners, stamped with their private seals, and sent to the Joint Examination Committee for evaluation. Schools not subject to random examination will have the principal supervise the teachers of each subject in evaluating the papers.

The sealed papers must not be opened until after the careful review and scoring are completed.

Within five days after the random examination, schools subject to random examination should prepare and submit to the Department of Education the grades of each student in each subject for each academic year, according to the table format below. (Table omitted: usual performance grades in each subject.) (Note: The average grade of the three academic years should be filled in for each subject.)

If a student who should participate in the random examination is temporarily unable to take the examination due to illness or special circumstances, the school may submit a request in accordance with Article 11, Section 2 of the revised regulations for the high school student graduation joint examination.

The method for calculating the results of the random examination in each subject will be carried out in accordance with Article 4 of the Ministry Order No. 5244.

Schools subject to random examination will be notified one day before the random examination after the chief examiners designated by the Department of Education arrive.

These methods are established and implemented by the Department of Education.

Various Commemorative Days: Commemorative Ceremonies Have Regulations; The Municipal Bureau of Education Orders All Schools to Pay Strict Attention and Not to Violate Regulations by Taking Unauthorized Holidays 178

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education issued an order to all public and private schools at all levels in the city yesterday, stating, "Upon investigation, there are clear central government regulations as to which commemorative days should be holidays and which should not. This bureau has also listed these in the academic calendar, which has been promulgated and implemented. However, the public and private schools at all levels in this city are inattentive to this matter and often arbitrarily take holidays based on hearsay, which is extremely inappropriate. Furthermore, commemorative days have either celebratory flag-raising ceremonies or half-mast flag lowering for mourning ceremonies, and these are often disregarded. This not only violates the intent of the central government but also damages the national dignity and must be corrected. It is hereby ordered that all schools pay strict attention to the matter of holidays and commemorative ceremonies for various commemorative days." This order.

Short Selling in Gold Market Intensifies; Premium Breaks 30 Yuan Mark 186

Central Bank Intervention Calms Market; Scattered Short Positions Gradually Increase

The gold market was initially affected by the continued rise in exchange rates and the strengthening of the US dollar. Large speculators, seeing the unfavorable environment, actively bought, causing prices to rise. In the morning, it was said that overseas silver markets in the UK and the US were flat. Traders predicted that after the market closed, there would be sellers at listed prices, while buyers would be below the listed price of 0.0625. The forward silver price in Monterey remained unchanged. Exchange rates continued to rise, and the price of raw gold in London fell by three pence. Off-exchange trading opened at 32.5 to 33 yuan. Dadecheng, Fuxing, Yongfutai, Yongyuanmao, and Yonghuixiang sold, but prices retreated to 31.5 yuan. Chunyuan Yong and others took advantage of the low prices to buy, stabilizing the market slightly. When the Central Bank announced its exchange rates, the UK and the US were flat, and the customs gold unit fell by 0.04 yuan. The standard gold premium was listed at 1142.2 yuan, and the market officially opened. There was much fluctuation after the opening. Later, because of the closing of positions by many parties such as Huixiang, Yicheng, Dingkang, Fuxing, and Yong, and the increased short selling by Yuanmao Yong, the 30 yuan mark was broken. The US exchange rate also eased, falling to a low of 28.5 yuan. It was rumored that the Central Bank intervened with 700 gold bars at a price of 29 yuan, which boosted the buying sentiment of large speculators. The price gradually rose above 30 yuan, and the market stabilized. However, due to the occasional pressure from the short side, there were many fluctuations despite the rise. At noon, the trend was hovering. The total number of chips currently is estimated to be over 14,000 bars, with the short side exceeding the long side by five firms. Chinese Merchants Continue to Sell

Net Increase/Decrease of Stored Cotton

—Survey on May 8th—

Heavy Import of Foreign Cotton 191

According to sources, 53,000 bales of Indian cotton arrived in April, and another 50,000 bales are expected to arrive in mid-May. There are also many arrivals of American cotton, creating significant pressure from foreign cotton. This is something that must be carefully considered. Regarding the supply and demand of cotton in this city, due to the government's implementation of cotton improvement policies, imports of foreign cotton have gradually decreased since 1930. Last year, imports of American and Indian cotton were only a fraction of what they used to be, indicating that self-sufficiency may be achieved soon. This year, foreign cotton speculators have increased their purchases compared to last year. The pressure from these imported cottons will further depress the market.

American Cotton: Old Crop Rises, New Crop Falls 192

Yesterday, American cotton opened with gains of 4 points and losses of 2 points across different months. Early in the morning, domestic traders bought old cotton, and foreign firms also made purchases, strengthening the market. However, cotton farmers then started selling aggressively, causing long positions to close. There was rain in Oklahoma and Texas, and the wheat market was weak, leading to a price decline. Domestic traders covered their May positions, while stockpilers sold at 11.57 cents. Subsequently, domestic traders bought July positions, while external demand was quiet and current demand sluggish. Spot prices rose by 2 points, while futures rose by 2 points to fall by 5 points. English cotton spot prices rose by 2 points, while futures fell by 12 points. Indian cotton initially rose due to short covering but weakened due to unfavorable Liverpool news. Bengal rose by 0.75 to 1 rupee, Oomra rose by 0.50 to 0.75 rupee, and Broach rose by 1 to 1.25 rupees. (Reported by telegram on the 8th)

Piece Goods: Smuggling Hinders Cotton Cloth Sales 194

—Only Gray Fabric Business Gradually Increases—

The cotton cloth market is very sluggish due to weak actual sales and the adverse effects of yarn and cotton prices. The reason for this is that smuggling of cloth from South China and North China has blocked the sales of Shanghai cloth, which is a major key. Both white and colored goods are overstocked and there is a risk of surplus. Yesterday, customers from Wuhu and Anqing in Anhui Province, as well as Wenzhou and Taizhou in Zhejiang Province, purchased slightly over a hundred pieces of colored and fine cloth. Sales of dyed cloth were slightly better, and the gray fabric business gradually increased. Yesterday, local dyeing factories continued to purchase 100 bales of Yufeng 12-pound Longtou fine cloth for this month, at a price of 6.85 yuan per piece. The Nanyang Company purchased over 60 pieces of Donghuo 13-pound Yiniu Tou coarse cloth, 11-pound blue and white fine cloth, and 10-pound Tiaowu market cloth.

Silk and Tea: Foreign Firms Actively Selling Silk 195

Overseas silk prices are improving daily, and the market is entering a normal trading pattern. Furthermore, European and American silk weaving factories are about to start production, and the demand for raw materials is gradually increasing. Therefore, yesterday, foreign firms in the local silk market resumed active trading. White silk of 13-22 strands, foreign re-reeled silk, and futures trading for June/July delivery were the most popular. Prices generally rose slightly. The total transaction volume was 180 bales (details in the Market Conditions section). Moreover, Shanghai sent out many silk telegrams yesterday, approximately 500-600 bales. It is understood that the prices offered by manufacturers are 800 yuan for 11-13 strands of white silk, 760 yuan for 13-15 strands, 650 yuan for 20-22 strands, and 680 yuan for 20-22 strands of foreign re-reeled silk. These prices are not far from overseas prices, so it is expected that the silk market may be even smoother next week.

Harvesting of New Wuyuan Tea Approaching Completion 196

This year, new Wuyuan tea was harvested one week earlier than usual due to the advice of various mountain households. Currently, harvesting in the eastern areas of Xitou, Longwei, Shangtan, and Xiaoqi is nearing completion. The tea picking work in the northern areas will also be finished soon. The products are very tender, and the amount of old and coarse tea has been greatly reduced compared to previous years. In terms of quantity, general merchants estimate that there are only 42,000-43,000 boxes. However, only a few tea shops, such as Shenyuan, Shengchang, and Sheng, are open to lending funds for the tea trade in this area, while most others remain cautious. Judging from the current situation, it is hoped that the opening price of new tea will increase.

European Sales of Chunmee Green Tea Still Strong 197

Yesterday, the green tea market continued to be robust. More than 130 boxes of new Chunmee samples displayed by various tea shops were all purchased by companies such as Xiehe, Tongfu, Baochang, and Hua Tea. Local Zhuang-grade hand-picked tea opened at 105 yuan, while ordinary Zhuang-grade tea opened at 93 yuan, with prices trending firm. It is said that a large batch of new goods will be launched next Monday.

Grains: Short Covering; Wheat Futures Selling Pressure Stronger in the Afternoon 198

Yesterday, the wheat futures market opened lower and continued to decline. The weather was good all day, and people in the interior generally expected a small harvest. Moreover, foreign wheat prices were reported to be 30-40 cents lower, and outside stockpilers were also wavering, prompting aggressive short covering. Selling pressure was even stronger in the afternoon, causing the market to fall further. Closing prices were down 4-5 cents for both near and distant months. Spot wheat was dragged down by the standard wheat, also down 5 cents yesterday. The total volume cleared by factories was over 4,000 bags, with Shandong wheat opening at only 5 yuan and Tongzhou wheat at only 4.87 yuan.

In the American wheat market, heavy rain in the Southwest, unprecedented this year, is expected to continue. Many long positions were closed, and both factory and external markets were weak, with prices likely to continue falling.

Children's Supplement

A Word to the Nation's Children on Purchasing Aircraft to Celebrate a Birthday 202

— Yongyu, Student of Minsheng Elementary School

"Aviation to save the nation" is a resounding slogan. Although the results are not bad, they are still not entirely satisfactory. My dear children, you have probably seen the news in the newspapers about purchasing aircraft to celebrate a birthday, haven't you? It is Premier Chiang's 50th birthday this year, and the people of the nation have the heroic act of purchasing aircraft to celebrate his birthday. This matter is very relevant to national defense. The ancients said that the rise and fall of a nation is the responsibility of every citizen. Although we are young, we are all members of the Republic of China. We should all get up and save money on sweets and snacks to contribute to this grand event. In major cities, many children spend more than one yuan on sweets every month. I believe that if every child in the nation donates two cents of sweets money each month, it won't be a big deal. However, many grains form a tower, and many bits of fur make a robe. If there are 50 million children in the nation, and each donates two cents per month, we can get one million yuan per month, which can be used to purchase ten aircraft. In one year, we can get over a hundred aircraft. If you save two cents of sweets money each month, it won't hurt you at all. However, by working together, the country will benefit greatly. Children, let's all get up and do it!

Student Self-Government Movement in Elementary Schools 203

— Zhuying

Recently, I read a publication from an American elementary school, which included an article about the self-governing life of elementary school students in that school. The United States is a democratic country with a highly developed democracy, and the people are all capable of self-government. In fact, in the United States, not only adults are capable of self-government, but we can also see from this record that American children are also capable of self-government. Indeed, only when there are children who can govern themselves can there be adults who are good at governing themselves. I think that the descriptions in this record are worthy of introduction to my country's children, so I have extracted and translated a few sections below.

Reading Club—The school's library is entirely managed by students. Under the library system, there are three reading clubs, divided into groups A, B, and C. These three groups are divided according to the level of their studies. The expression of their reading achievements is a meeting every two or three weeks. At the meeting, those who have gained insights from reading can go on stage and make a ten-minute report, which is judged by eleven pre-selected judges (students from different groups), each giving a separate score. At the end of the semester, the scores are tallied, and the person with the most points is ranked first. Another method is to take notes. At the end of the semester, the notes are evaluated by publicly elected judges. The names of the top two students in each group are entered in a special "Model Reader's List" book, which is permanently preserved in the library.

Athletic Association—This association is also entirely organized by students. Under the athletic association system, there are hiking teams, ball teams, calisthenics teams, and health and hygiene patrol teams. These small organizations require further explanation. The hiking team aims to collect specimens, held three times each semester, always on weekends. The ball team is mainly football, with two teams organized in each grade. One team is drawn from the two teams to form a grade team to play inter-grade matches. Every weekend, there are at least two matches. Health is measured by physical improvement and chest expansion. Checked once a month.

Service Club—This is a Boy Scout organization. But the scope of their service is very broad. In addition to the ordinary services in the corps, they are also responsible for monitoring the actions of their classmates. If they see a classmate doing something immoral and do not advise or report it, they will be severely punished once exposed. But those who have excellent grades or special achievements will also have their names inscribed in a "Model Scout List" book that will be permanently preserved.

I think that the children of our country should also organize these three items on their own, govern themselves automatically, and train to become good citizens of the future.

Thermos 204

— Zhen

One Sunday, Miner's father bought a thermos from the market. Miner saw the words "Keeps hot for 24 hours, keeps cold for 48 hours" written on the bottle. He was very surprised to see the seven words "Keeps hot for 24 hours" and asked:

"Dad, how can this thermos keep hot for 24 hours?" "What is it made of inside? Can you take it apart and show me?"

His father took the bottle apart and saw a snow-white small bottle. He said:

"Miner, look, this small bottle is made of double-layered glass, and the wall of the bottle is silver-plated. Because the bottle is double-layered, the air between the two layers is completely extracted to create a vacuum. Why vacuum? I'll tell you in a minute." Then his father took off his hat, took a sip of tea, and said: "As for how it can keep hot, there are some small reasons. Let me start from the beginning to make you understand better: When it comes to heat, there are three ways to transfer heat: Conduction: If you take an iron rod and put one end of the iron rod in the fire, after a while, the end you are holding will feel hot. This is called heat conduction. Convection: Liquids and gases rise when heated, and the cold parts fall, which is called heat convection. Radiation: After the above two methods, if there is no third method, there will be a big problem. If you see a light bulb when it is on, we can touch the light bulb and feel very hot. What is this reason? We know that the light bulb is empty, and there is no convection effect. It is not connected to the filament, so there is no conduction effect, which is the third way to transfer heat.

"As for how the thermos can keep hot for 24 hours? Because it avoids the three ways of heat transfer: The small bottle in the thermos is alone in the center and does not connect with anything, so there is no conduction effect. It is a double-layer wall, and the air in the wall is extracted, which can prevent heat convection. The wall is plated with silver, and when radiant heat touches it, it is reflected back. So with these three methods, hot water or ice water can be kept at its original cold or hot temperature in the bottle."

"Dad, what is the use of the pointed head at the bottom?"

"Because the air between the walls has to be extracted, and after the air is extracted, it is plugged here."

Little Science Problems

Why Don't Birds Get Electrocuted When They Sit on Power Lines? 205

— Zixi

As long as we pay a little attention when running on the road, we can see many birds hiding on the power lines, chirping and singing freely. It's strange that people get electrocuted when they touch the power lines, but birds don't get electrocuted when they hide on the power lines? To understand this principle, we should first know how we get electrocuted? We can observe from electric lights, electric stoves, and other electrical things that there are always two wires connected behind them. In other words, any electrical effect must have two wires connected at the same time. Electricity originally has the distinction between positive electricity and negative electricity or positive electricity and negative electricity. When there is an electrical effect, both of these types must be connected. Having only positive electricity is not enough, and having only negative electricity is not enough. Electrocution is also a type of electrical effect, so naturally it also requires two types of electricity. The reason why birds don't get electrocuted when they sit on power lines is because they only sit on one line. If they touch two wires, naturally we can't guarantee that they won't be in danger. However, in reverse: Why do we people sometimes get electrocuted when we touch one wire? The reason is very simple: Because although one hand only touches one wire, the two feet are on the ground, and there is another wire on the ground that people can't see. With two wires, you will naturally get electrocuted. However, we can avoid this danger by wearing a pair of rubber shoes.
